Please don't bash me as I'm putting my opinions in a very respectful way.  As much as I love them, the vocal arrangements in the song just isn't well done. Each of them sound passable at the very least with 2 of the members actually sounding quite good (I won't say who), but the arrangement just made them sound so off and incompatible with each other. Not to mention the autotune is too obvious for some members and it makes them sound kinda robotic, not in a way that sounds like it fits the song either. The arranger did not do them justice but the instrumentals are a vibe atleast.  In my opinion this song is in the last place for NijiEN's debut songs. Could've been done better.  Edit: further clarified my points

Stuck in brain wont leave, but i like it
Definitely one of the better songs nijisangi has put out. The production is mostly good, but the production on the vocals is just a little bit off. They don't use the pitch correction right, and it's just bad. Mind you, I love the autotune/cher/T-pain effect, but only when it's done right, and here its not done that great. Which is a shame, because the tone color of most of the singers is actually pretty good. A few people are undersinging, but for the most part, and for the size of this nijisanji group, you guys seem to be doing pretty well vocally,  so it's a shame that the production messed it up. But otherwise, the production is good, and so is the songwriting. And finally, decent lyrics!! I mean they're fine, it's no bjork, (nor is it trying to be, and that's ok) but some of the lyrics of the past gens were just soo awful. All in all, a solid 4.5/10 for me, definitely a song of all time.
